# Ticket board ‚ÄĒ step 2 (proving Theorem 1.2 from the axioms)

Source of truth for the proof phase.  Rationale, DAG, conventions, and wave schedule:
[`step2-plan.md`](step2-plan.md).  The **step-1 board** (statement formalization, ticket IDs
`T-xx` cited in module docstrings) is archived at [`tickets-step1.md`](tickets-step1.md).
Difficulty: ‚≠ź easy ¬∑ ‚≠ź‚≠ź medium ¬∑ ‚≠ź‚≠ź‚≠ź hard/design-sensitive.  Model: **F** = Fable
(design-heavy), **O** = Opus (well-specified).  Status: ‚ėź open ¬∑ ‚óź in progress ¬∑ ‚ėĎ done.

Rules: **no new `axiom`s without explicit user approval** (census at 13 ‚ÄĒ B10 added by explicit decision, P-06 escalation; B9 base-generalized + B11 added by explicit decision, P-15 escalation, user-approved 2026-07-03; **B11 split into B11a `hilbertSymbol_normCriterion_finiteDyadic` + B11b `unramifiedQuadratic_units_are_norms` by P-23, census 12‚Üí13, user-approved 2026-07-04** ‚ÄĒ `dyadicNormCriterion` kept as a same-name theorem, spectral-norm bridge isolated as a `def IsUnramifiedQuadraticSpectral`, not an axiom); statement tickets add their sorried theorems to
`SORRY_ALLOWLIST` in `scripts/check_axioms.sh` (same commit, entry cites the ticket), proof
tickets remove them; every ticket's new theorems satisfy `#print axioms` ‚äÜ std-3 ‚ą™ the ticket's
**Ax** column; `GQ2/Foundations/Axioms.lean` is frozen; sessions claim a ticket by marking its
row ‚óź before starting.  Paper: `paper/A_Profinite_Presentation_for_G__Q_2.pdf`.

every `t^k ‚Č† 1` has zero fixed space (**`fixedPoints_zpowers_tame_eq_zero`** ‚ÄĒ generalizes `fixedPoints_tame_inertia_eq_zero`: conjugates of `t^k` are powers of `t^k`, `‚ä§` killed by `hfaith` instead of `hram`), so the geometric sum vanishes (**`sum_range_orderOf_smul_eq_zero`**), and for `ŌČ`-fixed `v` the transversal sum `w := ő£_{k ‚Č† 0, k.val < (qk).val} u^{k.val}‚ÄĘv` (val-comparison picks one element of each pair `{k, qk}` ‚ÄĒ canonical, no choice, no induction) satisfies `w + ŌČ‚ÄĘw = ő£_{k‚Č†0} u^{k.val}‚ÄĘv = v`; so `ker(1+ŌČ) ‚äÜ range(1+ŌČ)` and `#V^ŌČ ^2 ‚Č§ #ker¬∑#range = #V` by first-iso counting (`AddSubgroup.card_eq_card_quotient_mul_card_addSubgroup` + `QuotientAddGroup.quotientKerEquivRange`).  **Statement amendment (documented)**: `involution_fixedPoints_sq_le` gained `hs1 : 1 ‚Č§ s` ‚ÄĒ the leaf was FALSE as previously stated for `s = 0` (`ŌČ = g‚āÄ^0 = 1`; Fully constructive, ~620 new lines, no `ūĚĒĹŐĄ‚āā`, no structure theorem, no finiteness in the splitting: `őĹ := ő≥+1` has `őĹ^{2^s} = 0` and group-sum `= őĹ^{2^s‚ąí1}` (squaring induction, no Lucas); given a full-depth `v‚āÄ`, a functional `őĽ` with `őĽ(őĹ^{2^s‚ąí1}v‚āÄ)=1` makes `T := ŌÜ‚ąėj` (coefficient map ‚ąė orbit map) `= 1 + (őľ+1)B` with `(őľ+1)^{2^s}=0` ‚üĻ **explicit geometric-series inverse** ‚üĻ `ŌĀ := T‚ĀĽ¬Ļ‚ąėŌÜ` retracts `j`, one regular block splits equivariantly, recurse (bound inherited); no full-depth vector ‚üĻ kernel-filtration bound collapses `V = 0`.  **`sylow_free_of_ramified` is now PROVED** from it (cyclic Sylow toolbox + tame relation transported along `c`); the residual sorry is the pure **counting inequality `card_fixedPoints_pow_le_of_ramified`** (`#V^P ^ |P| ‚Č§ #V` on a ramified simple faithful module) ‚ÄĒ no ‚ąÉ-iso content left.  Paper cross-checked (pp. 29‚Äď30 read this session): the criterion replaces the two Lean-hostile steps (Clifford induction over `ūĚĒĹŐĄ‚āā`; faithfully-flat projectivity descent) by their rational counting shadow.  ūĚĒĹ‚āā-rational plan for the inequality banked in the file section docstring: √©tale `ūĚĒĹ‚āā[‚ü®ŌĄ‚ü©]` factor fields + single-`C`-orbit faithfulness (cyclic `‚ü®ŌĄ‚ü©` has characteristic subgroups) + the O‚āā-linchpin (a `P`-stabilizer element acting `K`-linearly centralizes `‚ü®ŌĄ‚ü©` ‚üĻ abelian normal closure ‚üĻ nontrivial normal 2-subgroup ‚üĻ `FoxH.lemma_5_12` vs faithfulness) + finite-field semilinear fixed-point descent (additive Hilbert 90 / normal basis) ‚ÄĒ a recorded deviation from the paper (which uses 1-dimensional `ūĚĒĹŐĄ‚āā`-weight lines); de-risks the remainder from 'Clifford over `ūĚĒĹŐĄ‚āā`, poor Mathlib support' to explicit finite-field linear algebra.  New gotchas banked: numeral `rw` motive failure at `(2 : Module.End (ZMod 2) M)` (the polymorphic `one_add_one_eq_two` pattern catches the `2` in `ZMod 2`'s instance chain ‚ÄĒ pin with an explicitly-typed `have` first); `Fin.cons` on a constant family needs `(őĪ := fun _ => M)` everywhere; a single `rw [AddEquiv.apply_symm_apply]` rewrites all identical occurrences (a second copy errors).  **Reduced to the involution (Opus, 2026-07-06, std-3, Ax ‚ąÖ for the reduction): `card_fixedPoints_pow_le_of_half` + Jordan-increment concavity land.**  The counting bound `card_fixedPoints_pow_le_of_ramified` is now PROVED from a strictly smaller leaf `involution_fixedPoints_sq_le` (`#V^ŌČ ^ 2 ‚Č§ #V` for the involution `ŌČ = g‚āÄ^{2^{s-1}}` of the cyclic Sylow-2), via the standard elementary-abelian / Chouinard reduction, all constructive: **`finrank_ker_pow_succ`** (`dim ker őĹ^{k+1} = dim ker őĹ^k + dim(im őĹ^k ‚äď ker őĹ)`, rank-nullity for `őĹ^k : ker őĹ^{k+1} ‚Üí im őĹ^k ‚äď ker őĹ`) ‚áí **`finrank_ker_pow_concave`** (the increment `dim(im őĹ^k ‚äď ker őĹ)` is antitone by `finrank_mono` on `im őĹ^{k+1} ‚Č§ im őĹ^k`); two `‚Ąē`-lemmas **`seq_double_le`** (concavity's automatic `b(2m) ‚Č§ 2 b m`) and **`seq_first_increment_le`** (two equal `m`-term antitone sums are termwise equal ‚áí all increments flatten, `Finset.sum_eq_sum_iff_of_le` + squeeze); and **`card_fixedPoints_pow_le_of_half`** wiring them to `b k := dim ker(nuOp g‚āÄ)^k` with the card‚ÜĒfinrank bridge (`Module.card_eq_pow_finrank`, `ZMod.card`), `b(2^s) = dim V` (`nuOp_pow_card_eq_zero`), the freshman `nuOp(g‚āÄ^{2^t}) = (nuOp g‚āÄ)^{2^t}` (`genOp_pow` + `add_pow_two_pow_of_two_eq_zero`), and the ŌČ-fixed-points ‚ÜĒ `ker` count.  So `#V^ŌČ ^ 2 ‚Č§ #V` (the involution) + concavity force `2^s¬∑dim V^P = dim V`, i.e. the full bound.  `#print axioms`: the reduction is Ax ‚ąÖ; `sorryAx` enters `lemma_6_11` only through `involution_fixedPoints_sq_le`.  **The residual leaf is now the single-involution case** ‚ÄĒ quadratic descent (additive Hilbert 90) rather than a cyclic-group weight-orbit analysis; a much smaller finite-field-linear-algebra target. ## Per-ticket acceptance criteria

Common to all: `lake build GQ2` green; `scripts/check_axioms.sh` green (allowlist edits per the
rules above); `#print axioms` of every new theorem ‚äÜ std-3 ‚ą™ the **Ax** column; docstrings carry
paper eq./¬ß cross-references; new files, own board row only.

- **P-01** ‚ėĎ: `docs/STATUS.md` regenerated to the current tree (it stops at 2026-07-02); a script or
  Lean file (`scripts/axiom_ledger.*` or `GQ2/AxiomLedger.lean`) that reports, for every theorem in
  `GQ2`, its non-std-3 axioms, diffable against the per-ticket **Ax** declarations.  Re-run
  instructions in the file header.
  *Done.* `GQ2/AxiomLedger.lean` ‚ÄĒ a `run_cmd` metaprogram over the elaborated environment
  (`Lean.collectAxioms` per decl; robust to `namespace`/`private`, which the shell
  `.claude/tools/lean4/check_axioms.sh` cannot see).  Re-run: `lake env lean GQ2/AxiomLedger.lean`
  (header documents it; **not** imported by `GQ2.lean`, so `lake build GQ2` never runs it).  Output:
  per-B-axiom consumer lists (diff vs App. D ¬ßC), the `sorryAx` gap map, and an **ALARM** count for
  any other non-standard axiom.  Current run: 613 tracked decls, 601 at std-3, ALARM 0; only B7 has
  consumers (its 6 Euler stress tests), gap map = 6 (the 3 root sorries + 3 transitive).
  `docs/STATUS.md` rewritten as a per-layer ledger (axiom layer, 3-sorry gap map, def-layers
  T-05‚Ä¶T-18, proved infra), with verify-from-scratch commands.
- **P-02** ‚ėĎ: sorry replaced; **zero sorries in `Reconstruction.lean`**, allowlist entry removed,
  `exists_contSurj_of_card_le`/`reconstruction_of_equinum`/`reconstruction` all `#print axioms` =
  std-3 (`lean_verify`'d), `check_axioms.sh` green (census 10).  Level sets nonempty+finite via
  `contSurj_quotient_nonempty_finite`; the compatible family via `konigFunctor : OpenNormalSubgroup
  (ProfiniteGrp.of R) ‚•§ Type` + `nonempty_sections_of_finite_cofiltered_system` (K√∂nig), as the
  recipe said.  **Deviation from the recipe's assembly step**: instead of building a cone over
  `ProfiniteGrp.diagram R` and `isLimitCone.lift`, the section is assembled by an **elementary**
  embedding `e : R ‚Ü™ ‚ąŹ_U R/U` (closed embedding, `R` compact/`Q` Hausdorff) + **two Cantor
  intersections** (`IsCompact.nonempty_iInter_of_directed_nonempty_isCompact_isClosed`): one in `R`
  realizes each compatible family as `e r` (‚áí `Ōą := e‚ĀĽ¬Ļ‚ąėő¶` a continuous hom), one in `S` gives `Ōą`
  surjective.  **Why**: the `ProfiniteGrp.diagram` objects carry the discrete `‚ä•` topology, not
  `R/U`'s coinduced (equal but not defeq) topology, and `(diagram R).obj U` won't even synthesize a
  `TopologicalSpace` when used as a bare `ContinuousMonoidHom` codomain ‚ÄĒ so the categorical
  cone/lift route fights Mathlib's `CompHausLike`/`FiniteGrp` coercions at every step.  The
  product-embedding route stays in natural quotient topologies throughout.  Reusable spinoffs (top
  of the file, `open CategoryTheory`): `projMap`(+`_mk`/`_surjective`/`_id`/`_comp_apply`) and
  `konigFunctor` ‚ÄĒ for **P-04/P-05** (also over `OpenNormalSubgroup (ProfiniteGrp.of _)`).
- **P-03**: `FreeProfiniteGroup X` is t.f.g. for finite `X` (the generators' images topologically
  generate ‚ÄĒ density of the free group in its completion); t.f.g. passes to `profiniteQuotient`;
  instantiate: `GammaA` t.f.g. in the exact `‚ąÉ s : Finset _, ‚Ä¶` form `main_presentation` consumes.
  *Done (`GQ2/FinitelyGenerated.lean`, std-3):* predicate `IsTopologicallyFinGen G` (unfolds to the
  raw `main_presentation` form); `IsTopologicallyFinGen.of_surjective` (transfer along a continuous
  surjection ‚ÄĒ `DenseRange.topologicalClosure_map_subgroup`); `isTopologicallyFinGen_freeProfiniteGroup`
  (finite `X` ‚ÄĒ `ProfiniteGrp.ProfiniteCompletion.denseRange` + `FreeGroup.closure_range_of`);
  `gammaA_isTopologicallyFinGen` + `gammaA_topologicallyFinitelyGenerated` (the raw `‚ąÉ`-form P-19 feeds
  to `main_presentation`).
- **P-04** ‚ėĎ: (i) `tameRelator`/`wildRelator` of `univMarking` lie in `NA` (each dies in every
  admissible quotient ‚ÄĒ `map_*Relator_eq_one_iff` + `IsAdmissibleU`); (ii) the closed normal
  closure of `{x‚āÄ, x‚āĀ}`-images in `őď_A` is pro-2 (`IsProP 2`, via `MaxProP.lean`'s
  characterization: every open normal subgroup of `őď_A` pulls back to an admissible-dominated one ‚ÄĒ
  the Lemma 2.1 subdirect-closure argument).  Design note documenting the limit argument.
  *Done (`GQ2/AdmissibleLimit.lean`; every theorem `#print axioms` = std-3; no allowlist changes ‚ÄĒ
  pure proof ticket).*  Deliverables: (i) `tameRelator_mem_NA`/`wildRelator_mem_NA` +
  `quotientMk_*Relator_eq_one` (relations (5)/(6) hold in `őď_A`); (ii) `wildCore` (the closed
  normal closure `‚ü®‚ü®x‚āÄ,x‚āĀ‚ü©‚ü©`, on the raw quotient `F‚āĄ ‚ßł NA` ‚Č°ŠĶąŠĶČŠ∂† `GammaA`) with
  `isProP_wildCore : IsProP 2 wildCore`.  **P-05 interface**: `isAdmissibleU_iff_NA_le`
  (admissible opens = opens above `N_A`) and `generates_univMarking_map` (generation is automatic
  in every finite quotient ‚ÄĒ density of `FreeGroup` in its completion).  Engine (design note in
  the module docstring): `isAdmissibleU_top` (trivial quotient admissible ‚ÄĒ nonvacuity without
  App. B) + `isAdmissibleU_inf` (Lemma 2.1 subdirect closure, elementwise 2-power form
  `isPGroup_normalClosure_image_inf`) ‚áí directedness ‚áí compactness domination
  (`exists_isAdmissibleU_le`, the `proPKernel`-style argument) ‚áí `isAdmissibleU_of_NA_le`
  (Lemma 2.2 pushforward).  Lean gotcha recorded: state `wildCore` on `F‚āĄ ‚ßł NA`, not
  `Subgroup GammaA` ‚ÄĒ mixing the `‚Ü•GammaA` and raw-quotient spellings breaks instance search
  (`Membership`-instance mismatch), while everything is defeq on the raw type.
- **P-05** ‚ėĎ: the bijection `ContSurj GammaA G ‚ČÉ {t : Marking G // t.Admissible}` for finite discrete
  `G`: forward = push `univMarking` (admissible by P-04 + Lemma 2.2 `map_admissible`); backward =
  `quotientLift` along `NA_le_ker` (T-21); round-trips via `univMarking_map_toHom` and topological
  generation (P-03).  `Nat.card` conclusion in exactly `main_presentation`'s `hőďA` form.
  *Done (`GQ2/Prop23.lean`; zero sorries; `prop_2_3` and all helpers `#print axioms` = std-3).*
  Headline: `prop_2_3 : Nat.card (ContSurj GammaA G) = admissibleCount G` via
  `contSurjEquivAdmissible` (assembled from named halves `Marking.push`/`Marking.descend` with
  `push_admissible`, `descend_surjective`, `push_descend`, `descend_push`).  Key new lemma:
  `admissible_of_NA_le_ker` ‚ÄĒ the **converse of `NA_le_ker`** (surjective + `N_A ‚Č§ ker` ‚áí pushed
  marking admissible, via P-04's `isAdmissibleU_of_NA_le` + Lemma 2.2 transfer along
  `quotientKerEquivOfSurjective`); together they characterize admissible markings of `G` as the
  continuous surjections `F‚āĄ ‚Ü† G` killing `N_A`.  **Deviations from this sketch**: (i) t.f.g.
  (P-03) is *not needed* ‚ÄĒ the round-trip uses the **uniqueness half of the universal property**
  (`Marking.toHom_univMarking_map`: every `f : F‚āĄ ‚ü∂ P` is `toHom` of its own pushed marking;
  CMH-level form `toHom_hom_univMarking_map` via `ConcreteCategory.ofHom`, whose constructor is
  the public route ‚ÄĒ `ProfiniteGrp.Hom.mk` is private); (ii) the equiv is stated on `F‚āĄ ‚ßł NA`
  (defeq `GammaA`, the P-04 spelling convention), `prop_2_3` itself on `GammaA`.  Lean gotchas:
  prove uniqueness by `rw [Marking.toHom, Equiv.symm_apply_eq]` then rewrite
  `homEquiv_apply` **before** `fin_cases i <;> rfl` (otherwise `rfl` unfolds the completion
  adjunction ‚ÄĒ deterministic timeout), and keep the equiv's fields as *named* lemmas ‚ÄĒ inline
  `by`-blocks inside the `Equiv` literal retrigger the same timeout via nested-proof abstraction.

  distinguishes **tracked** files (current behavior ‚ÄĒ FAIL) from **untracked** ones (`git
  ls-files` membership): untracked violations print a clearly-labeled **WARN** block and do not
  fail the gate (rationale: the gate certifies the committed library; a parallel session's
  mid-flight scratch must not block everyone's commits ‚ÄĒ review fixes ¬ß5).  (ii) Scratch
  convention documented in `step2-plan.md`'s conventions: prototypes importing repo modules go
  in the session scratchpad or a root `scratch/` (gitignored), not `GQ2/`; if under `GQ2/`
  anyway, expect WARN noise.  (iii) Self-test: a planted untracked sorry file WARNs without
  failing; a tracked violation still FAILs (test, then delete the plant).  Gate: guard green on
  the current tree; the script diff reviewed against parallel allowlist edits (reconstruct from
  HEAD).
